msg:Hello fellow travelers! I recently stayed at a hotel in the city center and wanted to share my experience, which had a mix of positives and negatives. Initially, the hotel had a pleasing appearance, but unfortunately, the overall service and cleanliness left much to be desired.

Upon arrival, I encountered a chaotic scene at the front desk, with a lot of noise and commotion. This continued during the check-in process, which was quite bothersome. Once I entered the room, I noticed a pleasant view, but my disappointment grew when I realized that the room wasn‚Äôt adequately cleaned. To make matters worse, I discovered that the toilet paper roll provided was clearly used and not new. This was completely unacceptable and a clear violation of cleanliness standards.

Furthermore, I encountered issues with the shower head. It didn‚Äôt function properly. In addition, the shower head and fixtures were covered in limescale, indicating a lack of maintenance and attention to detail.

To add to the list of disappointments, the scale provided in the room for weight measurement was non-functional. This was an inconvenience, especially for those who rely on accurate weight measurement during their travels.

I believe it‚Äôs crucial for hotels to prioritize cleanliness, maintenance, and guest satisfaction. Discovering a used toilet paper roll, encountering a faulty shower head, and experiencing a non-functional scale were major letdowns.

On a more positive note, the hotel‚Äôs breakfast was average, nothing exceptional. Since I‚Äôll be staying in Chengdu for two more days, I decided to switch to another hotel. Regrettably, I won‚Äôt be considering this hotel for future stays.

I hope this feedback will serve as an opportunity for the hotel to address these issues and improve their overall service, cleanliness, maintenance, and attention to detail. As travelers, it‚Äôs important for us to share our experiences to encourage better practices in the industry.

Wishing you all safe and pleasant travels!

#FALtravel

Service:

I never thought that I was very lucky today. I had a smooth meal without queuing, so I came to the hotel nearly an hour in advance. I thought I came early and might have to wait in the lobby for a while before checking in. After the hotel staff Xiao Jin learned about the situation, he quickly communicated with the aunt who cleaned the guest room, so that I could check in smoothly without waiting. The experience was very good. I am very grateful for Xiao Jin's service!

Environment:
It was actually quite hot in the afternoon, but the hotel's central air conditioning was very powerful, and the hotel's sound insulation was good, which made my originally impetuous heart quickly calm down. I studied efficiently for several hours in the hotel in the afternoon, which was very satisfying.

Facilities:
The delivery I ordered was delivered to the door of the room by a robot, which was efficient and fast. Thumbs up

In general, it was a very satisfying stay experience. Thanks to Xiao Jin's service, this will still be my first choice for weekend accommodation
